Current Commentary

The Future Before the Suspension of Hostilities

— All

Since the outbreak of the conflict in Suiyuan, the entire nation, from top to bottom, has been holding its breath, focusing its attention on the changes in this new development. This is because Suiyuan is a crucial gateway for national defense, akin to a vital passage. It has long been viewed as a target of desire by ambitious individuals, who have been plotting to achieve their sinister schemes of conquest. If we fail to maintain it and allow it to fall, a single misstep will lead to complete failure. If the lips are gone, the teeth will be cold. Regret will be too late. Therefore, we must gather the strength of the entire nation and act swiftly to confront this crisis. Currently, General Fu Zuoyi, Chairman of Suiyuan, is responsible for guarding the northern gate. Fu is known for his tenacious resistance and defense. His performance in the Battle of Zhuozhou earned him widespread acclaim and lasting respect. Now that he is standing on the front line of national defense, applying his resolute and brilliant strategies to deal with the rebellious bandits, his past achievements alone are enough to inspire the people and boost morale. Moreover, at this critical juncture of survival, the soldiers are filled with hatred for the enemy and a shared sense of purpose. Their remaining strength is worth buying, and they will annihilate the enemy quickly. Even thousands of miles away, it is not difficult to imagine the heroic and resolute spirit of the soldiers at the front.

Furthermore, what we find comforting in this situation is not just the eager anticipation for the soldiers at the front. The local officials sacrificing their homes to alleviate the crisis and the common people enthusiastically following with food and supplies all demonstrate the arousal of patriotic sentiment, a stark contrast to the indifference of the past. Driven by the idea of national salvation and survival, whether they are brave warriors eager to fight or weak individuals holding on to what little they have, they all yearn to contribute and harbor grand aspirations of sacrifice. The formation of this will is sufficient proof that we are unwilling to surrender. Under the pressure of repeated constraints, the trend of mutual support has emerged. No matter how weak a nation may be, it cannot afford to dwell on short-term complacency. Historically, when border officials heard of alarms, their first priority was to demand military expenses from the central government. While such requests were indeed necessary, the accounting was often unreliable. Now, Yan Xishan, the Pacification Commissioner of Shanxi and Suiyuan, took the lead, following his mother's instructions, donating 870,000 yuan to supply the military. He was followed by Wang Jingguo, who contributed 40,000 yuan, Fu Zuoyi, who donated 50,000 yuan, and Zhao Daiwen, who gave 15,000 yuan. Others, such as Xu Yongchang, Sun Chu, and Yang Cheng Yuan, also generously pledged donations of varying amounts, demonstrating their dedication to defending the territory and their willingness to sacrifice their homes to alleviate the crisis. They are all keenly aware of the increasingly serious situation and deeply understand that without a resolute determination to fight to the death, it will be difficult to even preserve the most superficial aspects of the nation. Therefore, they have resorted to this last-ditch effort, demonstrating their unwavering commitment to defending the territory and resisting foreign aggression. As for the nationwide enthusiasm for supporting the border regions and the frequent assistance provided, both large and small, it is not driven by government orders or any external incentives, but purely by the surge of patriotic fervor and a sense of self-preservation. It is like hands and feet protecting the head and eyes, a spontaneous and unstoppable outpouring. Some even go without food to show their determination, enduring hunger and cold to express their sympathy. All of this demonstrates the people's deep concern for the situation in Suiyuan and their desire to ensure that no effort is spared.

With the commanders at the front so calm and dedicated and the people in the rear so enthusiastically supportive, who would believe that we cannot defeat a disorganized group of bandits? The repeated changes in tactics by the bandits and the repeated claims of non-involvement by a certain party are likely due to their awareness of our nation's vibrant spirit and the soldiers' determination to fight to the death, forcing them to adopt a more cautious approach. However, based on past experiences, we deeply understand that without a comprehensive and well-planned strategy, it will be difficult to develop our defensive capabilities. Even if the soldiers of Shanxi and Suiyuan are determined, their efforts are limited to local areas. How can they sustain this over a long period? We must mobilize troops from all sides and provide a continuous stream of supplies to completely eliminate the pervasive bandit atmosphere. Recently, we heard that the situation in eastern Suiyuan is developing, and the central government troops preparing to go to Suiyuan are actively moving towards their destination. If this is true, then our deep anxieties can be relieved. How excited will the soldiers in the trenches awaiting the enemy be when they hear this news?

Soviet Russia's Another Reactionary Case Verdict: One German and Eight Russians Sentenced to Death; German Consul Implicated During Secret Trial; Germany Indignant and Considering Retaliation

(Moscow) The military tribunal of the Supreme Court today announced the verdict in the anti-government case, sentencing German Streckling and eight Russian accomplices to death. Streckling had previously admitted during the trial that he had been in contact with a German spy in Moscow a few months ago, planning to destroy a coal mine. Observers believe this is similar to the Vickers Company employee case in 1933. Whether Germany will retaliate is now a matter of general concern. (National Telegram, 2nd)

(Moscow) The foreign diplomat involved in the case of German engineer Stickling and eight Russians sentenced to death has now been revealed to be Groskopf, the former German consul in Novosibirsk, who has now been promoted to Consul General in Kiev. This matter was admitted by Shi during a secret trial, but its public release may cause serious diplomatic incidents. All nine defendants in this case will be executed by firing squad and their property confiscated according to the current verdict. (Reuters, 22nd)

(Berlin) Officials here are awaiting the final report from German Ambassador to Moscow Schulenburg regarding the death sentence of German engineer Streckling in the Soviet Russian court in Novosibirsk before deciding on necessary actions. Some diplomatic circles here believe that Germany and Russia will not immediately break off relations. (Reuters, 23rd)

Main Text of the Verdict

(Moscow) The main text of the verdict in the case of the Trotskyist counter-revolutionary sabotage group at the Kemerovo mine in the Soviet Union is as follows:

"The preliminary investigation and trial records of the court confirm that the Trotskyist counter-revolutionary sabotage group engaged in criminal activities, establishing organizational links through Trotskyist members Noskov and Drobnis. Drobnis was one of the leaders of the Western Siberian Trotskyist secret organization, and his case will be tried separately. At the same time, organizational links were also established through Beigehanov and Sticklin, a German engineer at the Kemerovo mine and a defendant in this case, and Alimontov, who left the Soviet Union in 1935. The group's purpose was to undermine socialist construction and restore capitalism. They identified their primary task as carrying out sabotage activities to resist the Soviet state. They were directly guided by the Western Siberian Trotskyist Counter-Revolutionary Center, especially by Trotsky's confidants Mura Lov and Drobnis, who received instructions on carrying out sabotage and terrorist work from Pyatakov, Trotsky's closest aide and a member of the All-Union Trotskyist Center." The verdict then describes the group's destructive and criminal acts in the mine, stating, "The defendant, German engineer Sticklin, after receiving orders from a foreign intelligence agency, established a relationship with Beigehanov, whom he knew to be a saboteur, in 1934. With the aim of disrupting the management of the Kemerovo mine, he systematically instructed Beigehanov on sabotage tasks, delaying the construction of the Severnaya mine and undermining the development of the Telnaya mine. Sticklin proposed strengthening activities to Beigehanov to achieve greater results from the sabotage and, to this end, organized a counter-revolutionary sabotage group. This sabotage task was jointly carried out by Beige and other members of the Trotskyist counter-revolutionary sabotage group. In addition, Sticklin himself used sabotage methods to drill several mining holes in an attempt to obstruct the development of the mine and thereby disrupt coal mining. After being removed from his position at the mine, Sticklin instructed Beigehanov to continue the sabotage and even ordered him to explode the mines simultaneously. He also systematically reported his sabotage activities to representatives of a foreign intelligence agency.

Therefore, the crimes of Beigehanov, Noskov, Andreyev, Subin, Liashenkov, Kulov, Leonenko, and Kovalenko have been proven. They were members of the Trotskyist counter-revolutionary sabotage group at the Kemerovo mine and, under the direct leadership of the Western Siberian Trotskyist Center, carried out activities that endangered the Soviet state, in violation of Articles 58, 7, 9, and 11 of the Criminal Code.

The crime of Sticklin has also been proven. While serving as a mine supervisor at the Mailov mine, he accepted orders from a foreign intelligence agency. From 1934 to 1935, he repeatedly carried out sabotage activities himself and with the help of Beigehanov and other members of the counter-revolutionary sabotage group, intending to disrupt the work of the Kemerovo mine, which belongs to the Kuzbasugul, due to its economic and defense significance. He has violated Articles 58, 7, and 1 of the Criminal Code. Based on the aforementioned facts, the Military Tribunal of the Supreme Court of the Soviet Union sentences Noskov, Subin, Kulov, Liashenkov, Andreyev, Kovalenko, Leongenko, Beigehanov, and Sticklin to be shot and all their private property confiscated. This verdict is final and cannot be appealed to the Review Court." (Tass, 23rd)

German Reaction

(Berlin) It was announced here today that German Ambassador to Russia Schulenburg has again written to the Soviet Russian government, requesting that the defendants be given sufficient time to file an appeal. Shi's death sentence has aroused anger throughout Germany. The official German news agency even called the Soviet Russian action a "terrible repressive measure." (Reuters, 22nd)

(Berlin) It was learned here today that the German Embassy in Moscow has notified the Soviet Russian government that the charges against German Streckling of conspiring to sabotage and engage in espionage are unbelievable and demanded his immediate pardon. Newspapers here today reported that the trial was an unprecedented and unwarranted frame-up in the international community. The Soviet Russian action was nothing more than an attempt to create unrest in Europe. The German ambassador's request will be backed by the entire German nation. Germany will never allow its citizens to be falsely accused by a party-controlled judiciary. Furthermore, the Soviet Russian action was merely an attempt to blame others for the failure of its economic plans. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Syria Still Tense

Disturbances broke out in the Syrian capital Tripoli the day before yesterday. The rioters even set up defenses in the city center, exchanging gunfire with the military police. Although the sound of gunfire has stopped after the military surrounded the area, the tense situation in the city has not eased. The cities of Beirut and Saida are peaceful. (Havas, 23rd)

Japan's Budget for Next Year Compiled; Totaling 3.04 Billion Yuan; An Increase of 730 Million Yuan Compared to This Year; Army Budget 720 Million Yuan; Navy Budget 680 Million Yuan; 980 Million Yuan in Public Bonds to be Issued

(Tokyo) The Japanese Army and Navy ministries have accepted the reduction of 102,000,000 yuan and 98,000,000 yuan respectively from their draft military budget for next year. The Ministry of Finance has decided to submit the national budget for review on Friday. The total amount may be reduced by 3,040,000,000 yuan compared to the requests from various ministries. However, the projected revenue is only 2,200,000,000 yuan, leaving a significant shortfall. It is said that 840,000,000 yuan in public bonds will be issued to make up the difference. (Reuters, 23rd)

(Tokyo) The most difficult hurdle in the budget for next year, the budgets of the Army, Navy, and Agriculture and Forestry ministries, was decided in outline on the 22nd. After the Ministry of Finance organizes the figures and sends them to print, it will be submitted to the cabinet for approval on the 27th. The budget for next year has become a massive amount of 3.04 billion yuan due to the increase of 223 million yuan in local finance grants for the Ministry of Home Affairs. This is an increase of 730 million yuan compared to this year's budget of 2.31 billion yuan. (Domei, 23rd)

(Tokyo) The basic army budget decided yesterday is 330 million yuan. The second national defense plan in the new budget request includes 200 million yuan for next year's expenses, 180 million yuan for the Manchurian Incident, and 10 million yuan for general expenses, totaling 720 million yuan. The total cost of the second national defense plan is 2.7 billion yuan, of which 200 million yuan for next year's expenses will be used to enrich combat data, expand the air force, and improve the troops stationed in Manchuria. The six-year plan has been approved by the Ministry of Finance. (Domei, 23rd)

(Tokyo) After overnight negotiations between the Ministry of Finance and the Navy and the Navy budget meeting on the 23rd, the navy budget for next year has been decided at a total of 680 million yuan (total budget request of 770 million yuan), an increase of 130 million yuan compared to this year's budget. The navy is generally satisfied because the Ministry of Finance has fully approved the completion year of the third replenishment plan, the root of the navy budget for next year, and the continuing expenses for subsequent years. The outline of the navy budget for next year is roughly as follows (unit: 1,000 yuan):

(1) Baseline budget: 430,000, including 180 million yuan for the final year of the second replenishment plan.

(2) New requests: 250,000, including 150 million yuan for the year of the third replenishment plan. (Domei, 23rd)

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Finance's original plan for the 1937 budget has been decided by the Ministry of Finance meeting, namely the public bonds to be issued next year. The total amount of general and special accounts will reach 980 million yuan, which is quite close to the maximum limit of 1 billion yuan for current public bond digestion capacity explained by Finance Minister Baba in a special meeting. The huge amount of 980 million yuan in public bonds issued is unprecedented in Japanese financial history. Its contents include 830 million yuan for general accounts and 150 million yuan for special accounts, an increase of 127 million yuan for general accounts and 73 million yuan for special accounts compared to the 1936 budget. (Domei, 23rd)

(Tokyo) The content of the budget for next year decided by the government yesterday is as follows (in units of 1 million yuan):

Total budget: 3,040

Ordinary revenue: 2,200

(Ordinary revenue is divided as follows:)

Basic revenue: 1,590

Increased tax revenue: 423

Natural increase: 60

Increased tariff revenue: 40

Pre-approved surplus: 10

Increased cigarette price revenue: 25

Special account surplus: 61

Public bond revenue: 830

The budgets of the Army, Navy, and Agriculture and Forestry ministries decided on the 22nd are as follows:

Army: 720

Navy: 680

Agriculture and Forestry: 130

(Domei, 23rd)

(Tokyo) The compilation of the budget for next year, which was expected to be difficult to resolve, proceeded unexpectedly smoothly. The unprecedentedly large budget of 3.04 billion yuan can be resolved at the budget cabinet meeting on the 27th without the need for political compromises, as in previous years. As a result, the government is relieved. However, the government will make every effort to resolve outstanding issues. For example, the four-minister meeting on the reform of the central administrative organization will temporarily continue to adjourn after the third meeting decides on the outline of the state policy establishment agency because it is necessary to compile the budget. Starting next week, it will be re-evaluated and discussed in conjunction with the five-minister meeting. In addition, the parliamentary system investigation committee, which caused an uproar due to the Army Minister's attendance, and the House of Peers system investigation committee, which held its first general meeting, will officially begin discussions from next month. It can be seen that the political situation will enter a busy period as the end of the year approaches because of the imminent convening of the parliament. (Domei, 23rd)

Spanish Civil War Raging; New Struggle Arises Among Nations; Germany and Russia Increase Warships to the Mediterranean Sea; Italy and Germany Deny Sending Submarines to Aid in Battle

Constantine: The tense situation of international intervention in the Spanish Civil War is increasingly worrisome today. According to a radio announcement from the Bilbao government in Spain, the Soviet government has sent 35 warships to the Mediterranean Sea to protect Russian ships. Prior to this, the rebels had announced a blockade of the port, and it was rumored that a Soviet Russian merchant ship had been sunk by the Spanish rebels. (National Telegram, 22nd)

(London) Italy and Germany have both denied reports that the submarines that attacked Spanish government warships in the port of Cartagena belonged to Italy and Germany. A German naval officer in Berlin told a Reuters reporter, "There is no trace of German submarines in Spanish territorial waters." Rome has also officially denied that the submarines belong to Italy. (Reuters, 23rd)

Brest: It was learned today that three German warships sailed to the Mediterranean Sea on Sunday. (National Telegram, 23rd)

(London) German Ambassador General Ribbentrop met with Prime Minister Baldwin at 10 Downing Street for 45 minutes yesterday. In the evening, the cabinet suddenly convened a meeting. Foreign Secretary Eden also went to Downing Street, spoke briefly, and returned to the Foreign Office to meet with the Spanish ambassador. It was reported that the ambassador informed him that he had received a telegram from the Madrid government stating that foreign submarines had bombed Spanish government warships. The French ambassador also visited Eden at the Foreign Office. (Reuters, 23rd)

(London) Ambassador Ribbentrop reportedly stated that Germany still pursues a policy of non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War and will continue to cooperate with the Non-Intervention Agreement Adjustment Committee. (Havas, 23rd)

Madrid: The Aviation Ministry has issued a communiqué stating that several submarines suddenly attacked government warships anchored at the entrance to the port of Cartagena in the southeast yesterday. The cruiser Cervantes was damaged, but the Monte Lauro was not hit. Since the rebels have no submarines, these submarines must belong to foreign fleets. (Havas, 23rd)

Valencia: According to a semi-official statement here today, Mallorca is now virtually a territory of Italy, used as a base to supply the Nationalist army with weapons to attack mainland Spain. The Nationalist army currently has 10,000 regular troops stationed on the island and has forcibly recruited 25,000 men to form a fascist army, commanded by Italian officers and equipped with Italy's latest weapons. Those who disobey orders are imprisoned or executed. Italian ships currently transport food and munitions to the island twice a week. In addition, fourteen Italian three-engine seaplanes and three destroyers are stationed in the port. (Reuters, 22nd)

(London) The Non-Intervention Agreement Adjustment Committee for the Spanish Civil War is scheduled to hold a meeting at 5:00 PM today. (Havas, 23rd)

Italian and German Chargés d'Affaires Have Arrived; Rebel Commander Pays High Respect

The flags of Italy and Germany were hung in the city to express welcome. The two Chargés d'Affaires are scheduled to go to Burgos tomorrow to take office. In the port of Barcelona, Catalonia Autonomous Region, in the northeast, Soviet Russian officers and technicians are actively setting up defenses, such as building new-style trenches and setting up barbed wire, to prevent the Nationalist army from attacking." (Havas, 22nd)

(Berlin) After the German government recognized the Spanish Nationalist army government, the military government appointed Tester Data, the original secretary of the German Embassy, as the chargé d'affaires to Germany. (Havas, 23rd)

(London) Price, a reporter for the Daily Mail, was recently dispatched to Rome and Berlin to interview dignitaries from both countries. Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano and several important German politicians have all made statements to him. Price summarized these statements and reached the following conclusion, stating that Italy and Germany will not hesitate to use force to assist the Spanish Nationalist army when necessary. He said, "The act of recognizing the Spanish Nationalist army government by Italy and Germany is attached with a promise, that is, if the Nationalist army is in danger of failure, the two countries will come out to assist it." (Havas, 23rd)

(London) The Times recently published a commentary on the recognition of the Spanish Nationalist army government by Germany and Italy, expressing deep concern about the consequences that this move may cause. It said, "Although the governments of Germany and Italy are still continuing to cooperate with the Non-Intervention Agreement Adjustment Committee for the Spanish Civil War, their rash actions are making it more difficult for the governments of various countries that are sincerely neutral in the committee. It would have been wiser for Germany and Italy to wait a little longer, at least until after the fall of Madrid, before proceeding with recognition. What the two countries have done now is less because of a thorough understanding of the situation and more because they are driven by emotion because of the same ideology. The effect is that if the Spanish Nationalist army fails to meet the expectations of Italy and Germany and fails to achieve victory, then the two countries' intervention in the Spanish Civil War will inevitably go further than it is now. This is where the crisis in the whole of Europe lies." (Havas, 23rd)

Spanish Rebels Close in on the Capital Center, Bombing with Artillery and Airplanes, Residents Flee Madrid, Unlikely to Occupy within Two Weeks

(London) This dispatch from our special Reuters correspondent with the Spanish Nationalist Army states that after sixteen days of bombing Madrid, the Nationalist Army has secured an important stronghold. However, there is little hope of quickly occupying the capital. Several front-line observers estimate that the Nationalist Army will have to fight for two more weeks before they can occupy it. (Reuters, 22nd)

Avila The Nationalist Army continued to make progress in their attack on Madrid on Sunday, but their advance was slow, as they had to occupy houses along the way in an orderly manner. It is reported that the Moorish soldiers have adopted special tactics for seizing houses. The first step is to rush into the ground floor of the house, then shoot into the ceiling to create large holes. Hand grenades are then thrown through the holes until the defenders withdraw. When encountering multi-story buildings, this method is used to occupy each floor until the entire building is cleared. This method has been used repeatedly and has been very effective, resulting in a significant increase in casualties. (Reuters, 23rd)

Madrid Suburbs Spanish Moroccan troops and foreign legionnaires occupied the northern suburbs of Madrid today. Street fighting with government troops occurred at the capital's sports ground, which is located there. The rebel forward command claims that the Capital Park has also been occupied, which is only two and a half miles from the center of Madrid. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Madrid The rebels are now very close to the center of the capital and can shoot at the Modelo Prison with machine guns. However, government troops have repelled the rebels in the north and are shelling the university district in the west and the rebel-held former royal gardens in the south. At 6:10 this morning, rebel planes flew over the capital again and carried out bombing raids. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Madrid Our special correspondent reports that a Nationalist Army plane flew over the capital this morning and dropped six or seven bombs in the central and northern districts, killing several civilians, including a child. (Havas, 23rd)

(London) The report that the Spanish cruiser Cervantes was damaged has been confirmed by the Central destroyer Grauw. According to reports, a massive explosion occurred on the cruiser, resulting in the ship listing and having to be towed into port for repairs. (Reuters, 23rd)

Madrid The Nationalist Army heavily shelled the capital today but without using airplanes. It is claimed that the attack tonight was quite successful. The Modelo Prison has been reduced to ashes. Currently, the most advantageous factors for the government forces are the cold weather and their tanks. The Moorish soldiers in the Nationalist Army are particularly afraid of the cold. Even when wearing heavy coats, they lack fighting spirit. Every night after dark, the Nationalist Army uses searchlights to illuminate the Manzanares River and the bridges over it to detect any government army tanks attempting to cross the river. The government forces now have loudspeakers installed on armored vehicles, with a range of up to six miles. They are often driven to the front lines to conduct various types of propaganda against enemy soldiers. (Reuters, 22nd)

Madrid Rebel artillery heavily shelled key locations in the capital today, and passenger cars at the North Station were shattered. Residents screamed in panic and scurried through the streets. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Madrid Almost all non-combatants will be evacuated from Madrid today to allow the defending forces to operate more freely and to provide some psychological relief. The scene of the refugees leaving the capital was extremely pitiful, as each had relatives and friends participating in the war and felt that this departure might be their last. (Reuters, 23rd)

Madrid Government officials are requisitioning various public vehicles today under rebel artillery fire, hoping to evacuate over 8,000 women, children, elderly, and disabled people from the city to the Prado Museum before midnight. It is estimated today that the number of civilians killed in the city has reached between 1,000 and 1,500, with about 3,000 wounded. Officials in charge of the evacuation say that if all the women, children, and non-combatants in the city were to be evacuated, the number would reach 200,000. They also said that government troops had recaptured the village of Nueva Carceda and the Velázquez building in the university district on Sunday. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Britain Decides to Use Warships to Protect Merchant Ships, While Planning to Prohibit British Ships from Carrying Munitions to Spain

(London) Foreign Secretary Eden announced in the House of Commons today that the government will introduce a bill in the House to prohibit British ships from carrying munitions to Spain. The British government advocates non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War and does not wish to grant the rights of belligerents at sea to either side in the Spanish Civil War at this time. Therefore, if necessary, British warships will protect British ships outside the three-mile territorial waters to prevent interference from any party. (Reuters, 23rd)

Barcelona The British cruiser Arethusa arrived here last Wednesday from Majorca and has now weighed anchor and returned to its origin. According to sources in London, the ship is now sailing to various ports along the Spanish coast, so its deployment has no special significance. The British destroyer Gallant is still docked in Barcelona, preparing to carry British citizens out of the country. (Reuters, 22nd)

(London) The Cabinet decided today to take important naval steps to protect British shipping when the Spanish rebels implement a blockade of ports. It is understood that this plan stipulates that British warships may escort merchant ships when necessary. The Cabinet also decided that neither the Spanish government forces nor the rebels may blockade ports and will notify Spanish rebel leader General Franco and the Spanish government of this decision tomorrow. According to reliable sources, Britain believes that both sides' blockades of ports are illegal because the principles of international law do not recognize either party in a civil war as a belligerent group, and both sides' blockades are merely empty words, as neither has sufficient warships to implement a blockade. (National Telegram, 22nd)

(London) The Cabinet held a meeting this afternoon, attended by Prime Minister Baldwin, Foreign Secretary Eden, Home Secretary Sir John Simon, Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain, First Lord of the Admiralty Sir Samuel Hoare, and Minister for Coordination of Defence Inskip. Today was originally a Sunday holiday, but the Cabinet was deeply concerned about the possibility of a major incident in the Mediterranean due to reports that the Spanish Nationalist Army was blockading and bombarding the port of Barcelona. Therefore, a special Cabinet meeting was held to discuss what methods to use to avoid international disputes. It is expected that Foreign Secretary Eden will attend the House of Commons tomorrow to officially announce the decisions made by the Cabinet. Political figures predict that the government may recognize the two parties involved in the Spanish Civil War as belligerent groups. (Havas, 22nd)

(London) Foreign Secretary Eden is scheduled to make a speech in the House of Commons this afternoon to explain the Cabinet's current policy on the Spanish Civil War. According to the Daily Mail, "The Foreign Secretary will definitely state that Britain does not intend to recognize the Spanish Nationalist government as a belligerent group, and therefore any actions by that government that attempt to blockade the port of Barcelona will constitute piracy." (Havas, 23rd)

(London) Regarding the issue of recognizing the two sides in the Spanish Civil War as belligerent groups, after the French ambassador, Corbin, visited the Foreign Office yesterday to express his opposition, official sources have confirmed that the British government has temporarily abandoned this proposal. Ambassador Corbin also visited the Foreign Office again this morning to discuss the precautionary measures that the British government should take in response to the threat by Spanish Nationalist leader General Franco to blockade the port of Barcelona. Foreign Secretary Eden also summarized the speech he is scheduled to deliver in the House of Commons this afternoon for Ambassador Corbin. In addition, the British government has issued instructions to its merchant ships stationed within Spanish territorial waters, the content of which will be announced by the Foreign Secretary in the House of Commons. (Havas, 23rd)

Hungarian Regent Goes to Rome, Accompanied by the Prime Minister and Foreign Minister

Budapest, Hungary Regent Admiral Horthy, accompanied by Prime Minister Darányi and Foreign Minister Kánya, took a special train to Rome via Vienna at 3:30 this afternoon. Political figures have officially stated that Horthy's trip shows that while Austria is pro-German, Hungary has pro-Italian tendencies. Although Horthy and most of his cabinet members are Protestants, this trip will also include a visit to the Vatican to express their respect for the Pope's authority. This is Horthy's second foreign trip since becoming regent. The first was in August of this year, when he visited Germany and Austria and met with Chancellor Hitler in Berchtesgaden, Germany. However, political figures believe that Horthy's trip to Germany at that time was unofficial, and his meeting with Hitler was merely a hunting trip, with only one staff member accompanying him. This trip to Rome, however, is an official visit, with the Prime Minister and Foreign Minister accompanying him. In addition to being officially hosted by the Italian government, he will also inspect the army in Rome and the navy in the port of Naples, which shows the importance of the visit. In addition, German Foreign Minister Neurath's previous visit to Hungary was also unofficial, while Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano's recent visit here was an official visit. This shows that the relationship between Hungary and Italy is different from the relationship between Hungary and Germany. In this regard, political figures also stated that Italy has twice supported Hungary's claim to revise the treaty, while Germany has only paid lip service and avoided getting involved. In short, the reason why Hungarian Regent Horthy is visiting Rome is that German officials have stated that they cannot support Hungary's claim and have been in contact with Hungary's enemies. (Havas, 23rd)

Famine Relief and Ceasefire Donations - Teachers and Students in Beiping Rise to Aid Suiyuan -

— Special Correspondence from Beiping

Since the outbreak of the war in eastern Suiyuan, people here, feeling the tragic bravery of our soldiers fighting on the front lines and their difficult circumstances, and in order to express the support of people in the rear for the loyal and brave soldiers who are determined to defend the territory, there has been a universal call for aid to Suiyuan. Among these calls, various spiritual and material manifestations are numerous. The three matters of fasting, ceasefire, and fundraising are the most moving and thought-provoking.

(1) Fasting: When the fasting movement was first proposed, some people still held doubts, thinking that this was a method used by prisoners to protest against certain treatments by prison officials. One example was seen in the past when Mr. and Mrs. Niu Lan requested to live together and were not allowed. Another example was seen this year when political prisoners in Tianjin Prison demanded an increase in food rations. As for the recent donation of aircraft and funds by prisoners in Xuzhou Prison, as well as the donation of funds to aid Suiyuan by prisoners in Yangzhou Prison, the method of saving money through fasting was also used, because they were imprisoned and had no money to donate, so they had to resort to this method, which should be considered separately. However, most students are well-off and can do their best to contribute, so there is no need to advocate a fasting movement, which would be excessive. The savings are not much, and it is harmful to health. However, the majority opinion is that material donations are certainly necessary, but in order to express the greatest determination, the fasting movement is the most effective. Although the savings of one person are not much, this is a simple and easy thing to do. All citizens can do it. If a trend can be created, out of the 450 million people, except for the soldiers at the front, everyone can fast for one day, and the amount obtained would be astonishing. Moreover, the greatest significance of this movement lies in the spiritual aspect. It can leave a very deep impression on the fasters, give great stimulation to the general public, and give unparalleled encouragement to the soldiers at the front. Therefore, its significance cannot be calculated by the amount of money saved. In the past few days, the latter's opinion has been widely agreed upon by the general public, so the fasting matter has been launched successively in various schools.

Up to now, nearly ten schools have fasted for one day each, and several schools have reduced their food to coarse food (such as corn buns) and remitted the remaining money to the front lines. This includes universities, middle schools, elementary schools, public schools, special vocational schools, and tutoring schools, all of which are available. In terms of age, from 30-year-olds to children around 10 years old, as well as regardless of gender, all participated, which is truly moving. In terms of past examples here, no movement has ever been so widespread. The depth of the Suiyuan war's inspiration can be seen from this.

Most of the students in various schools come from middle-class and above families, and they are usually well-fed and well-clothed. Once they fast, what state will their physiology and psychology be in? This is a highly noteworthy question. The reporter has visited various schools and talked with those who participated in the fasting. In most cases, the first meal of fasting only feels hungry. By the second meal, they feel empty in their stomach and weak all over. By the third meal, their bodies are weak, and bitter water constantly overflows their throats, wanting to vomit but unable to. At this time, if they drink more water or tea, the hunger will be even worse. If they don't drink, their stomachs will be too empty and extremely uncomfortable. In severe cases, they cannot fall asleep at night. According to a ten-year-old girl, when everyone was fasting until the second meal, she was so hungry that she secretly planned to use her saved twenty copper coins to buy snacks to satisfy her hunger, but she finally gritted her teeth and donated the twenty copper coins to the school's Suiyuan Aid Association. The reporter was moved when he heard this, but seeing her innocent and lively state, he could not help but smile bitterly. In terms of psychology, because this is due to patriotic enthusiasm, all participants were extremely excited at the beginning. By the second meal, they entered a state of calmness. By the third meal, a feeling of sadness arose spontaneously. Therefore, when they resume eating the next day, this impression is particularly deep and remains in their minds forever.

The money obtained from fasting and reducing food to coarse food in various schools has reached about a thousand yuan so far, but the spiritual harvest is by no means something that this small amount can represent.

(2) Ceasefire: Once winter arrives here, the normal climate temperature is around 0 degrees Celsius. This year's climate is slightly warmer than in previous years, but ice has already begun to form more than a month ago. Since the beginning of winter (November 6th), the climate has become more severe due to the north wind. On the 16th, it snowed heavily for nearly 12 hours from 1 am, and the accumulated snow on the ground reached several inches at noon when it stopped. All households in the city have already lit their stoves, because without doing so, it would be impossible to resist the cold. Knowing this, the severity of the pressure that the cold adds to the students after they hold a ceasefire movement can be generally seen. According to the usual practice of various schools, fires are started around the beginning of November each year and not extinguished until March of the following year. The fire period lasts about four months, and the daily consumption of coal in various schools, including classrooms, offices, and student dormitories, is quite considerable. This time, when the Suiyuan war broke out, the students were extremely excited. In addition to thinking of all possible ways to provide assistance in terms of material and spirit, they also thought of this kind of ceasefire movement that deprives the body of warmth, in order to save money on coal and remit it to the soldiers at the front.

After the ceasefire movement was proposed, it was immediately accepted by the students of various schools, who held it separately and obtained the consent of the authorities of each school. The ceasefire period ranged from two weeks to several days. During the period, all offices, classrooms, dormitories, and even dining halls and toilets in the school stopped using stoves. The entire school suddenly turned from a warm place into a cold world. The chimneys standing in the sky, which had been constantly smoking all day since the fires were lit, suddenly stopped, and the scene was extremely desolate. In the washrooms of various schools, the ditches for pouring water often had thin ice.

During the ceasefire period, the spirit shown by the students of various schools was exceptionally good. All regular work such as attending classes, reading books, etc. did not stop. No one was ever seen shrinking back due to the cold. And various activities to aid Suiyuan were intensified, and students from various schools actively participated. Male and female students all went out or stayed on campus to raise donations during the day, and in the evening, they held symposiums on campus or sewed cotton clothes for the soldiers at the front. All of this was carried out at temperatures around freezing, and they did not care about their hands and feet being red and swollen or their mouths and ears cracking. In the lively and enthusiastic atmosphere, there was infinite calmness and seriousness.

After the offices and classrooms stopped using fires, all the faculty and staff of the various schools were affected, but they were all very excited and never complained. The reporter once asked a professor of a certain school who was over seventy years old. At that time, he was sitting on a cold sofa in the faculty lounge, shivering. Seeing this was very pitiful. His ears were hard of hearing, and the reporter asked him several times in a very loud voice before he understood. Who knew that after he understood, he suddenly said sternly, "This is a matter of patriotism. Everyone can endure it, why can't I?" Although his tone was firm when he said this, his old body trembled even more. The reporter respectfully remained silent for a long time. According to statistics, the coal expenses saved by the ceasefire in various schools has reached several thousand yuan. Although the amount is small, it comes from depriving the faculty and students of various schools of their body warmth. This money is used to make cotton clothes, leather clothes, gloves, and other cold-weather items to give to the soldiers fighting in the icy and snowy conditions on the front lines, which also has a special meaning.

(3) Fundraising: Fundraising has been going on sporadically before the outbreak of the Suiyuan war. After the outbreak of the war, it changed from slow to rapid, and from unorganized to organized and planned. As of now, the fundraising methods that have been used include the following: (1) Fundraising from all students, faculty, and staff in the school; (2) Students forming fundraising teams to raise donations from pedestrians, shops, and households on the streets; (3) All faculty and staff initiating and donating one day's salary; (4) Female student groups organizing variety shows to donate the proceeds from ticket sales to the front lines. In addition, there are various fundraising methods under consideration, but they have not yet been adopted. Among the above methods, the third method is the most effective and has the largest amount of money. Each national university donates more than a thousand yuan per day. The second method is the next most effective. Wherever student fundraising teams go, most people enthusiastically contribute. As for those who truly do not give a penny, they are the minority of the minority. According to the results of the past few days, intellectuals are the most generous, followed by workers, then households, then merchants, and finally, small officials are the most stingy.

In short, in order to help the soldiers fighting at the front, the teachers and students of various schools here are doing their best to find ways to raise more funds. Although the local authorities here had a proposal to prohibit students from fundraising on the streets a few days ago, after the authorities of various schools contacted the local authorities and reached an agreement, remedies have been made for the various malpractices that the local authorities were worried about. Under the compliance with these various methods, the full-scale fundraising of students throughout the city will be launched on the 22nd. ... (5) Handling registration of rice merchants; (6) Investigating customs import and export certificates. C. The Second District Commissioner's Office may add personnel to handle the management and investigation of food affairs. The required expenses shall be drawn from the general reserve fund, with a temporary limit of 2,000 yuan, and the special office shall prepare a budget for review. (22nd)

Anhui Provincial Government Revises Regulations on Rice Export; Northern Anhui to Implement Warehouse System; Central and Southern Anhui to Centralize Visa Issuance and Release at Wuhu

Wuhu Correspondence: Anhui Province exported a total of 4 to 5 million shi of rice this year, a huge amount that exceeds the records of the previous five years. Recently, in order to promote sales to Guangdong Province as much as possible to restore the original market, the provincial authorities have repeatedly contacted the Guangdong Provincial Government by letter and telegram to discuss the exchange of Anhui rice for Guangdong sugar. Now Guangdong has sent Yan Zefang to Wuhu to investigate the production and sales of Anhui rice. Yan stayed here for two days and held several talks with representatives of the rice industry. He left by boat on the 22nd for Anqing to discuss implementation methods with the provincial government. However, after the provincial government issued a ban, all counties have acted vigorously. Hexian Yuxi Town, the general port for sailing transport, has successively detained hundreds of rice boats, and rice merchants have risen up to fight for release, but have not yet been allowed. However, the Wuhu sea route is still reporting exports as usual. The Fuhe and other rice shops recently handled more than 100,000 shi of rice to North China, which have all been loaded. There are still a large number of iron boats stopped on the surface of the water, busily loading. Since the customs has not received a notice from the Inspector General of Customs to ban transportation, it is still released as usual. Recently, it was heard that Min Cai and Jian Er Ying jointly proposed to the provincial government to revise the regulations on banning rice exports. The main points are: In northern Anhui, implement a warehouse system to handle storage and mortgages; in central and southern Anhui, concentrate on Wuhu to restrict exports, and issue visas by the commissioner of the second district for release. The plan has been resolved and approved by the provincial government committee meeting and is divided into three points: A. All areas in northern Anhui shall prohibit the export of grain at any time. In the future, the agricultural warehouse management office and the local banks in this province shall be ordered to promote the warehouse system as much as possible and handle storage and mortgages. Unless there are special circumstances, they shall not be forfeited. B. Regarding the food in central and southern Anhui, a restrictive principle shall be adopted. Gao Wenbo, commissioner of the second district, shall be responsible for handling it according to the following methods: (1) The commissioner Gao shall sign and release the food imported and exported in Wuhu; (2) Food merchants shall submit an application form for exporting rice. The application form shall be determined by the special office and reported to the government for filing; (3) According to customs statistics, a daily output quota table shall be prepared. If the quota is exceeded, appropriate restrictions shall be imposed; (4) On one hand, personnel shall be sent to the grain distribution points to investigate the need for rice and whether there are sales of rice. On the other hand, merchants shall be ordered to fill out an application form stating that the rice is for domestic sales only, and promising to be subject to legal sanctions if they violate the regulations.

Important Gold Mine Discovered in Fuzhou; Geological Survey Exploration Results; Extremely Rich Gold Mine Deposits Everywhere

Nanchang Correspondence: Jiangxi's mineral resources are extremely rich, such as tungsten in southern Jiangxi and coal in Pingxiang, which are famous in the world. It is learned that the Provincial Geological Survey has specially organized exploration teams to explore the mineral resources of the entire province separately. They have successively discovered many valuable mineral resources such as manganese, iron, and barite. According to a report from Zhou Daolong of the Linchuan Exploration Team in Fuzhou, several quartz vein outcrops were found on small hills in the Mopan Mountain Gan Jia Ling area of ​​the Yisu District, 40 miles northeast of the county seat. After breaking them open and examining them, they contained gold particles. At the moment, they explored the veins everywhere. From the road from the Hu family at the foot of the mountain to the Dagan market, they found more than 20 gold ore veins within four or five miles vertically and horizontally. They generally trended north at 20 degrees east, running parallel to each other with very steep dips. The wider ones were about one meter wide, and the narrower ones were several centimeters wide. The extension reached more than 500 meters. Gold can be seen with the naked eye in the outcrops, and its richness can be imagined. However, it contains a small amount of impurities such as pyrite and limonite. Samples have been obtained and transported to the province for analysis. The exploration team crossed the Ru River east from there to Yunshan Station, and heard that there were gold diggers near the station, so they expected that there must still be natural gold-producing areas upstream. The scope of gold production in Linchuan must be broad, and there will definitely be more important discoveries in the future.

Songjiang Yue Temple Digging Artesian Well

The residents of the wooden county town relied on drawing water from the city river for drinking, but the river water was turbid and unclean, which hindered sanitation. County Magistrate Li discussed and approved that various banks and money shops in the financial sector would advance funds, and first dig a well in the Yue Temple outside the city, and use the proceeds from selling water in the future to repay the advance funds. After several meetings, it was generally determined that the Shanghai Tianyuan Well Drilling Company would contract for it at a price of more than 2,000 yuan and was expected to be completed in 45 days. Yesterday, County Magistrate Li broke ground in front of the Ten Kings Hall in the Yue Temple on the west side and immediately started construction.

The rent for Huadao paddy fields in this county has been determined by the county government convening meetings of district chiefs and tenants every year. The rent for this year's paddy fields has been discussed and announced, with the highest amount being five dou and two sheng per shi, divided into four grades, and the lowest amount being four dou per shi. One sheng is especially reduced for disaster-stricken map shares.

Widow Dies from Abortion

Chen Shi, a widow in the fourth district of Yifu Township, has assets and was recently seduced by Zhou Pinru, a villager, and became pregnant. In order to avoid attention, Zhou sent someone to abort Chen, but the surgery was improper, resulting in her death. Chen's aunt filed a complaint with the county government, requesting redress. The dispatched law enforcement police went to the countryside in disguise and arrested the principal offender Zhou Pinru and the person involved, Gu Laotai, and sent them to the county jail. Later, Gu was allowed to be released on bail. Chen's body will be transported to the Zhenru Forensic Research Institute for examination in the near future, and then interrogated.

Suzhou Murder Case in Muduo

The Procuratorate of the Wuxian District Court reported that Zhang Changxiang, the local security chief of Jinshan Township, Muduo, reported that Liu Hesheng, a stonemason in the township, went out to work on the 21st and did not return until late. On the 22nd, his wife went out to look for him and found a pile of blood and a shoe near Chahubang. The shoe was indeed her husband's shoe, so she was shocked. Later, her husband's body was found in the river, with his hands tied behind his back, a huge stone hanging from his waist, and multiple knife wounds on his head and other places. It was believed that he had been killed and thrown into the river after being murdered by someone he had a grudge against. A request was made to send someone to examine the body. The local procuratorate sent prosecutor He to the township on the 23rd to examine the body, and the public security fifth sub-bureau in charge paid close attention to the case, investigated the case quietly, and arrested the murderer to bring him to justice.

Large-Scale New Movement Exercise

This county has held the New Movement Exercise and has conducted three trial performances, which have achieved good results. A large-scale exercise will be held at 6:00 pm on the 23rd. Land and water traffic will be stopped, and all students and soldiers in Suzhou will participate in the exercise. The lights will be turned off for two hours. At that time, the public will hear the echo of the siren and will all go indoors. New Movement instructors will fly planes to inspect the city for lights. Women's rescue teams and doctors must participate in the work. However, due to traffic and lighting reasons, all entertainment venues will temporarily suspend performances at night.

Wuxi Expand Suiyuan Aid Movement

In order to initiate the consolation of the soldiers fighting in Suiyuan, the county chamber of commerce of this county convened a meeting of representatives from various institutions, organizations, and schools yesterday to discuss expanding the Suiyuan aid movement. Qian Sunqing, chairman of the meeting, resolved (1) to expand the organization of the One-Day Contribution Advocacy Committee to concentrate will and increase strength; (2) to centralize all Suiyuan aid donations in the county, control them as a whole, and remit them to the soldiers resisting the enemy in Suiyuan; (3) the county party headquarters will be responsible for drafting methods, scheduling regular meetings of all sectors for practical implementation. Also, Lixin Cloth Factory and all staff and workers are willing to contribute their one-day income of 2,887 yuan, 1 jiao, and 8 fen to the country to fulfill their national duty. Also, Xicheng Long-Distance Bus Company donated more than 100 yuan, the brewing industry 100 yuan, and the Zhejiang Salt General Stack 123 yuan, all to console the soldiers.

Lack of Silkworm Eggs in Jiangsu and Zhejiang

In recent months, overseas silk markets have soared, and domestic silk merchants have all made profits of more than double. The future of the silk industry has embarked on a prosperous path. The silkworm farmers in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces are more interested in raising silkworms next spring than before. Therefore, the sales of silkworm eggs next spring will also be very smooth and there is already a trend of supply exceeding demand. According to Lu Zirong, a member of the Jiangsu Provincial Silkworm Industry Improvement Association, the spring seeds next year will be in great shortage. The silkworm eggs produced by the breeding fields in Jiangsu Province can only export 300,000 sheets, in addition to supplying the needs of the province. At present, 800,000 sheets of silkworm eggs have been imported from Zhejiang Province into Jiangsu Province. Therefore, according to the needs of silkworm farmers, Jiangsu Province will be short of 500,000 sheets of spring seeds. The situation of seed shortage in Zhejiang Province is even more severe than that in Jiangsu Province, with a shortage of 1 million sheets. Combining the two provinces, there is a total shortage of 1.5 million sheets.

Nantong Search and Suppress Bandits in Reclamation Area

In the Xinfeng Reclamation Area, the bandit leader Song Bingjiu has recently gathered more than 100 followers and colluded with pirates to carry out arson and robbery, which has caused great harm. Wu Ying, the captain of the second brigade of the Industrial Police, is leading a team to search and suppress them and has arrested the main criminals and handed them over to the district security headquarters for interrogation.

New Channel for Yangtze River Passenger Ships

Because the Qingtian Reef channel in the Tongzhou River surface is only ten feet deep, the Yangtze River passenger ships will temporarily stop calling in order to avoid danger. Traffic between the counties under the jurisdiction of Tongzhou and the ports on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River has been cut off, which is quite inconvenient. After surveying by the customs, a new channel has been discovered. It has already been located in the Yao port of the river and new black buoys have been set up. The Yangtze River passenger ships going up and down the river have been regularly berthed in Tong since the 22nd.

Change of Public Security Bureau Chief

Song Mingqi, the director of the Nantong County Public Security Bureau, was transferred with He Runzhang, the director of the Songjiang Bureau. He arrived in Tong on the 21st to take over the post and announced that Yang Deji and others were section chiefs.

Yangzhou Telegrams Province to Close Canals Along the Canal

The Huai River Diversion Committee, because of the dam being built to cut off the flow in Shaobo, Qiqu, Jiangdu, and preparing to open the ship lock, all of the canal mouths along the canal should be closed at the same time. After the dam is built, it will be opened again. A telegram was sent to the provincial government to transfer it to the Jiangbei Canal Works Bureau to inform the relevant counties to assist. It is heard that the local county government has received the notification and ordered the relevant district bureaus to comply.

Bar Association Re-election Unsuccessful

The fourth session of the autumn regular general meeting of the Jiangdu Lawyers Association, the election meeting, was held at 3:00 pm on the 22nd at the association in Quekou Street. After resolving various cases, a member, Fang Ren, made a temporary motion, based on the provisions of Article 12 of the constitution, that the president and vice president can only serve one term, and whether the problem of wheel-style mutual appointment can be discussed at the conference. The atmosphere at the meeting suddenly became tense, and members successively expressed their opinions and debated fiercely, each expressing their reasons. No solution has been found. Then the mountain supervisor and supervisor withdrew from the meeting to discuss a solution. An opinion was expressed on this issue and it was proposed to submit it to the provincial party headquarters for submission to the central government and to the Ministry of Judicial Administration for interpretation. The election would be held after the interpretation, so as to avoid the election being invalid. Therefore, the meeting on the 22nd was adjourned.

Fever of Salary Donation to Aid Suiyuan

The Jiangdu County Party Headquarters convened representatives from various institutions, organizations, and schools in the county at 2 pm on the 23rd to discuss the establishment of a National Contribution One-Day Income Movement Promotion Committee to facilitate the aid to Suiyuan. It was learned that all institutions, in addition to the county government staff and police who had donated one day's salary, and ordered the district offices to comply, Shu Guohua of the Construction Bureau also transferred 32 yuan and 2 jiao from one day's salary of all employees to the county for forwarding. Other bureaus and institutes were all donating and concentrating.

Gaoyou Flour Mill Preparing to Resume Business

Yuheng Flour Mill outside the north gate of the county is the largest enterprise in the county. It was founded in the early years of the Republic of China and has a very good business. The prosperity of the city depends on it. No less than two or three thousand people directly and indirectly depend on it for their livelihood. Unfortunately, since the levee was breached in the 20th year of the Republic of China, the mill was right in the path of the breach. Although the mill building was not washed away, the internal machinery and wheat flour were severely damaged. As a result, it has been closed for more than five years. During this period, there have been several attempts by people from Yangzhen to take over the factory, but they ultimately failed to reach an agreement due to improper conditions. It is now heard that the factory has been formally leased by Yicheng Flour Company in Zhenjiang and has hired workers to repair the houses and reorganize the machinery. It is expected that business can be resumed after the beginning of the year.

Xiaoshan All Sectors Console Suiyuan Soldiers

On the 21st, all sectors of Xiaoshan held a general assembly of all sectors to assist the Suiyuan guards and soldiers at the county party headquarters. Representatives from the gentry, business, school, and agencies participated unanimously. In addition to passing the fundraising to comfort, they also passed the letters and telegrams comforting the soldiers at the front, and the frugality of food donations to the government.

Letter Received

Editor,

I am writing to you because I recently read a news message on the eighth edition of the second sheet of your newspaper on November 17 of this year about the dismantling of the traitorous organization in Mingguang. Because the wife of Chen Juzheng, a gardener outside the county seat, often sells vegetables outside the store, it was mentioned that her husband had recently gone out and entrusted her to forward a family letter on his behalf, for a very short time. However, whether Chen is a traitor is unknown. It was not known until it was revealed. The First District Office inquired about the truth by order of the county government, but there was no arrest. Later, he was ordered to return. The statement of an organization for mutual communication of news is thought to be due to a distant rumor. I request that you make a correction. I respectfully ask for your peace.

Wang Zhiren

Representatives of the慰勞救護會 (Comfort and Rescue Association) Including Wang Xiaolai Departed by Plane Yesterday Morning to Beiping, First Staying Overnight in Xi'an, Then Flying to Taiyuan This Morning

The Suiyuan Bandit Suppression 慰勞救護會 (Comfort and Rescue Association), jointly formed by the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and three other groups, appointed representatives including Wang Xiaolai, together with Yan Fuqing and others representing the Shanghai Rescue 事業協進會 (Business Advancement Association), to fly to Xi'an and then to Suiyuan by special plane at 10:00 AM yesterday. Details are recorded below:

Yan's Telegram of Welcome

After the meeting decided to send representatives to Suiyuan for consolation, it first telegraphed Ge Xishan, the 綏靖 (Pacification) Director in Taiyuan. On the morning of the day before yesterday, they received a reply telegram of welcome from Yan, which read, "Thank you for informing us that you have united various groups in Shanghai to organize a Suiyuan Comfort and Rescue Conference, raising funds for assistance, and planning to visit our province to guide everything. We are deeply grateful and will express our welcome, eagerly awaiting your arrival to receive your instructions. Special telegram of thanks, Yan Xishan respectfully bows."

After the association received Ge's welcome telegram, it held a meeting the night before last, attended by more than ten people including Du Yuesheng, Qian Xinzhi, Wang Xiaolai, and Huang Renzhi. They telegraphed Yan and Fu that evening to report.

The funds are temporarily held by the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, and will be remitted as soon as the representatives send a telegram. Kong Xiangxi Donates 10,000 Yuan to Comfort Suiyuan Soldiers, All Sectors Enthusiastically Contribute

According to the Central News Agency, Kong Xiangxi, Vice-President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, donated 10,000 yuan of his personal funds through Yuhua Bank to the soldiers at the front lines, to encourage them in their brave resistance against the bandits in Suiyuan. Recently, Sheng Shengyi, Director of the 苏浙皖 (Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui) Regional Unified Tax Bureau, and his staff also donated 10,000 yuan, requesting that Minister Kong remit it to Chairman Fu. The original text of the telegram read, "Respected Chairman Fu Zuoyi of Suiyuan, Brother Yi, The bandits' invasion is a matter of universal indignation. Director Sheng Shengyi of the 苏浙皖 (Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui) Regional Unified Tax Bureau and his staff deeply admire your loyalty and courage, and the soldiers at the front lines are enduring extreme hardship, fighting the enemy in this freezing weather. They have jointly donated 10,000 yuan for the soldiers at the front lines to purchase leather clothing. We have remitted it and hope you will acknowledge receipt. Respectfully, Kong Xiangxi bows."

Employees of Two Railways

Incensed by the bandit invasion of Suiyuan, the colleagues of the Jinghu, Huhang, and Yong railways jointly convened a meeting led by the Party (Special Party Branch), government, and labor union leaders. They decided that all employees, regardless of their position, would voluntarily donate their salaries to comfort the soldiers at the front lines. The first batch of 10,000 yuan, representing half a day's salary for all employees, was handed over to the Shanghai Bank of China on the 18th to be remitted to Pacification Director Yan of Taiyuan, who would then transfer it to Chairman Fu Zuoyi. It is reported that both Director Yan and Chairman Fu have sent replies to the bureau. The telegram texts are as follows: (1) "To all gentlemen of the Jinghu, Huhang, and Yong railways, Chairman Fu Zuoyi of Suiyuan acknowledges receipt of your kind telegram. The bandit invasion of the border has aroused universal indignation. Our troops are defending the territory and killing the enemy, as is our duty. We are deeply grateful for your distant encouragement and donation of salaries. In addition to informing all soldiers at the front lines to encourage morale, we hereby send a telegram of thanks. Fu Zuoyi bows, followed by a secret code." (2) "To all colleagues of the Jinghu, Huhang, and Yong railways, Pacification Director Yan Xishan acknowledges receipt of your kind telegram. We have received the 10,000 yuan you donated to comfort the soldiers defending the Sui border. We are extremely grateful and have distributed it to Chairman Fu, and announced it to the front line comrades, who are all inspired and motivated to defend the territory to the death, hoping to repay the nation's expectations. Special telegram of thanks, Yan Xishan, followed by a secret code." It is reported that the bureau has decided to continue to donate another 10,000 yuan, totaling one day's salary.
